Abella < Set subgoals off.


Abella < CoDefine sim : p -> p -> prop by 
sim P Q := (forall A P1, {one P A P1} -> (exists Q1, {one Q A Q1} /\ sim P1 Q1)) /\
  (forall X M, {oneb P (dn X) M} ->
       (exists N, {oneb Q (dn X) N} /\ (forall W, sim (M W) (N W)))) /\
  (forall X M, {oneb P (up X) M} ->
       (exists N, {oneb Q (up X) N} /\ (nabla w, sim (M w) (N w)))).

Abella < CoDefine bisim : p -> p -> prop by 
bisim P Q := (forall A P1, {one P A P1} -> (exists Q1, {one Q A Q1} /\ bisim P1 Q1)) /\
  (forall X M, {oneb P (dn X) M} ->
       (exists N, {oneb Q (dn X) N} /\ (forall W, bisim (M W) (N W)))) /\
  (forall X M, {oneb P (up X) M} ->
       (exists N, {oneb Q (up X) N} /\ (nabla w, bisim (M w) (N w)))) /\
  (forall A Q1, {one Q A Q1} -> (exists P1, {one P A P1} /\ bisim Q1 P1)) /\
  (forall X N, {oneb Q (dn X) N} ->
       (exists M, {oneb P (dn X) M} /\ (forall W, bisim (N W) (M W)))) /\
  (forall X N, {oneb Q (up X) N} ->
       (exists M, {oneb P (up X) M} /\ (nabla w, bisim (N w) (M w)))).


Abella < Define nbisim : p -> p -> prop by 
nbisim P Q := (exists A P1, {one P A P1} /\ (forall Q1, {one Q A Q1} -> nbisim P1 Q1)) \/
  (exists X M, {oneb P (dn X) M} /\
       (forall N, {oneb Q (dn X) N} -> (exists W, nbisim (M W) (N W)))) \/
  (exists X M, {oneb P (up X) M} /\
       (forall N, {oneb Q (up X) N} -> (nabla w, nbisim (M w) (N w)))) \/
  (exists A Q1, {one Q A Q1} /\ (forall P1, {one P A P1} -> nbisim Q1 P1)) \/
  (exists X N, {oneb Q (dn X) N} /\
       (forall M, {oneb P (dn X) M} -> (exists W, nbisim (N W) (M W)))) \/
  (exists X N, {oneb Q (up X) N} /\
       (forall M, {oneb P (up X) M} -> (nabla w, nbisim (N w) (M w)))).

bisim_nbisim_absurd < apply to H13 H14.
Proof completed.

Abella < Kind o' type.


Abella < Type tt, ff o'.


Abella < Type conj, disj o' -> o' -> o'.


Abella < Type boxMatch, diaMatch n -> n -> o' -> o'.


Abella < Type boxAct, diaAct a -> o' -> o'.


Abella < Type boxOut, diaOut, boxIn, diaIn n -> (n -> o') -> o'.


Abella < Define sat : p -> o' -> prop by 
sat P ff := false;
sat P tt;
sat P (conj A B) := sat P A /\ sat P B;
sat P (disj A B) := sat P A \/ sat P B;
sat P (boxMatch X Y A) := X = Y -> sat P A;
sat P (diaMatch X Y A) := X = Y /\ sat P A;
sat P (boxAct X A) := forall P1, {one P X P1} -> sat P1 A;
sat P (diaAct X A) := exists P1, {one P X P1} /\ sat P1 A;
sat P (boxOut X A) := forall Q, {oneb P (up X) Q} -> (nabla w, sat (Q w) (A w));
sat P (diaOut X A) := exists Q, {oneb P (up X) Q} /\ (nabla w, sat (Q w) (A w));
sat P (boxIn X A) := forall Q, {oneb P (dn X) Q} -> (forall w, sat (Q w) (A w));
sat P (diaIn X A) := exists Q, {oneb P (dn X) Q} /\ (exists w, sat (Q w) (A w)).


Abella < Define neg : o' -> o' -> prop by 
neg ff tt;
neg tt ff;
neg (conj A B) (disj A1 B1) := neg A A1 /\ neg B B1;
neg (disj A B) (conj A1 B1) := neg A A1 /\ neg B B1;
neg (boxMatch X Y A) (diaMatch X Y A1) := neg A A1;
neg (diaMatch X Y A) (boxMatch X Y A1) := neg A A1;
neg (boxAct X A) (diaAct X A1) := neg A A1;
neg (diaAct X A) (boxAct X A1) := neg A A1;
neg (boxOut X A) (diaOut X A1) := nabla x, neg (A x) (A1 x);
neg (diaOut X A) (boxOut X A1) := nabla x, neg (A x) (A1 x);
neg (boxIn X A) (diaIn X A1) := nabla x, neg (A x) (A1 x);
neg (diaIn X A) (boxIn X A1) := nabla x, neg (A x) (A1 x).


Abella < Theorem neg_nabla : 
forall F G, nabla x, neg (F x) (G x) -> (forall W, neg (F W) (G W)).



============================
 forall F G, nabla x, neg (F x) (G x) -> (forall W, neg (F W) (G W))

neg_nabla < induction on 1.


IH : forall F G, nabla x, neg (F x) (G x) * -> (forall W, neg (F W) (G W))
============================
 forall F G, nabla x, neg (F x) (G x) @ -> (forall W, neg (F W) (G W))

neg_nabla < intros.


Variables: F G W
IH : forall F G, nabla x, neg (F x) (G x) * -> (forall W, neg (F W) (G W))
H1 : neg (F n1) (G n1) @
============================
 neg (F W) (G W)

neg_nabla < case H1.

Abella < Theorem neg_sat : 
forall P F NF, neg F NF -> sat P F -> sat P NF -> false.



============================
 forall P F NF, neg F NF -> sat P F -> sat P NF -> false

neg_sat < induction on 2.


IH : forall P F NF, neg F NF -> sat P F * -> sat P NF -> false
============================
 forall P F NF, neg F NF -> sat P F @ -> sat P NF -> false

IH : forall P F NF, neg F NF -> sat P F * -> sat P NF -> false
H1 : neg F NF
H2 : sat P F @
H3 : sat P NF
============================
 false

Abella < Theorem dist_form2 : 
forall P Q, ((forall F, forall X Y, sat (P X Y) (F X Y) ->
                  sat (Q X Y) (F X Y)) ->
                 false) \/
  ((forall F, forall X Y, sat (Q X Y) (F X Y) -> sat (P X Y) (F X Y)) ->
       false) ->
  (forall F, (forall X Y, sat (P X Y) (F X Y) -> sat (Q X Y) (F X Y)) /\

Abella < Theorem sat_match1 : 
forall P F X, sat P F -> sat (match X X P) F.



============================
 forall P F X, sat P F -> sat (match X X P) F
